The lighting and sound were much better than expected.  When other bands I want to see come here, I will be sure to go again.
1 BIG plus. < Text>
This venue just opened, the few bad comments below are completely off. There are snack carts everywhere. Security to get it was very easy as they had multiple metal detectors and people checking. Alcoholic drinks are what all Live Nation venues charge. Bottled water was only $3 not $4.
And so far the first band that finished up was amazing. Sound in here is fantastic.
I think this is an amazing place to have big name bands play.<//Text>

The staff were smiling, informative and helpful.  The bartenders were also smiling, engaging and did not 'short pour'.  Concert seats are padded and comfortable. < user_name>
Michael Snyder< /user_name>
<review>Nice venue with plenty of parking. Magnolia is walking distance to several restaurants if you want a pre-show dinner, and there is a large, full bar inside the theater. There are no bad views, any seat will do, but they are a little tight on leg room. The sound system was great. It was my very first time getting acrylic and gel nails. For my first experience I was willing to be accepting of how my nails would turn out to look. One thing I did want, was for the nail color in both my toe and hand nails to match. First, they were trying to convince not  get an acrylic on my toes ( i needed it though as I had foolishly cut them in a weird angle) The manicure was looking great until the color started setting. The gel color did not match my toes. I pointed this out to the manicurist. They insisted it was the same ( my nails on my hand were clearly a bright scarlet red, while my toes nails were of a burgundy/brown color). I pleaded with them to find  the matching color , they're answer, over and over again ( as they kept applying coat after coat) was that the polish read the same name as that of the one they had used on my nails. Apparently when using a gel color that has the same name as a regular nail polish, will be lighter and not the same as they kept saying ( I now know). They finally found one similar to match the color on my toes. I thought they would have wiped off  the red color off, but instead they just put another coat of "the right color" on top. I Got left with what looks like chunky nails. I did not like feeling as if I could not get what I wanted or was paying for. The prices for both a mani and  pedi are more expensive then what I am accustomed to compared to different nail salons I've been to. So, the reason for my three stars? It is a unique - small nail salon.The place was clean with beautiful and simple decoration. Perhaps if I would have kept the first nail color that was applied to my nails, I would have been ok with it, but again I wanted to get what I was paying for . I barely noticed how chunky the nail color looks on top of my acrylics when I got home.  I am willing to give my nails another chance with acrylics. Not sure if it will be this place again though. Would have really wanted them to wipe away that first color to show more professionalism  from a manicurist.</Text>

< text>
This is their flagship store for the region and is new after being opened a year or so ago. It's definitely aimed towards the home DIY and maintenance cried and not the building Trade.

It's got an amazing array of products, all of reasonable quality (but not convinced sometimes by the garden furniture section). Power tools, garden tools, paints, screws, bolts, storage, keys, plants, bathroom.... I almost always end up spending more money then I mean to :(

On holidays they have fun kids activities or the front or in the garden centre.

The loyalty scheme doesn't provide any significant discounts so don't rush to give them your personal info.</text>

< Review>
I avoided this place for a while because the prices seemed high, especially for whole pizzas. On "pi" day (3/14) we got a coupon for Pieology. The line was out the door, all day! Since we had planned on pizza for dinner we decided to go to pizza my heart instead. We were NOT disappointed! The prices are higher than your average chain (like Pizza Hut, Domino's, etc) but the quality is unmatched. Ingredients are super fresh, delicious and the crust is perfect. Service is also really good! Definitely recommend you stop by for a good slice or whole pizza. By the way, the large pizza is REALLLLLY large!!< /Review>

<rating>4<//rating><Review>I've been to Pizza My Heart a couple times now. I consider myself a big pizza fan, and I can get pretty excited about certain pizza places. I'm lucky in my hometown to have a large variety of different style pizza joints. There's one kind though that I feel is under represented and that's why I love visiting San Jose. I get excited for Pizza by the Heart because of a couple main things. The first thing I enjoy about this place is the size of the slices. These things are huge, and I think the average person can get a good meal with one slice, but you really need more than just one! The other thing I especially like about Pizza by the Heart is how messy these slices can be. You'll have grease dripping down your fingers, dripping down your chin.. it's a mess. I love it though, a huge greasy slice of pizza. Some might have an issue with the amount of grease or mess you get with these slices, but I love it.. many others do, this place can get pretty busy. I'm a creature of habit and always get the same type of pizza, so I can safely say pepperoni is good. The other flavours you'll have to see for yourself. One star deducted because it's really tough to do a perfect pizza. 4 stars is great though.< /Review>< Pictures>

< Text>
Pizza My Heart is one the best pizza places in DTSJ. The location is perfect if you're a student, or finishing up a day of shopping. The staff are friendly, competent, and capable. I was there last Friday. My girlfriend and I each ordered a slice. After the cashier discovered he had burned our pizza a bit, he apologized and offered the burned slices along with our new ones. That may not seem like a huge deal, but I was happy that he offered.

Eating in the restaurant is pretty standard. Unless the place is packed with students, the  volume never goes above a dull roar. The pizza is delicious (I reccomend the Big Sur if you've never tried it), and the prices are fairly reasonable. If you're in the area, it's definitely worth a try.< /Text>
